### Q46 — Full-universe top-of-book sweep (GOAL.md Phase-1 M2)
Status: DONE (2026-07-17, research loop) — `collection/universe_sweep.py` built (+16 new tests: 10 `tests/test_universe_sweep.py` + 6 `tests/test_hourly_pass.py`), read-only + unauthenticated over the public `/markets?status=open` listing, NO `series_ticker` (a genuine full-universe sweep), bounded at a `MAX_CALLS=20` cap. One append-only JSONL snapshot line per open market with raw top-of-book (`yes_bid`/`yes_ask`/`no_bid`/`no_ask` parsed from Kalshi's `_dollars` strings, L90) + at-touch sizes + `last_price` + `volume`/`volume_24h` + `open_interest` + `liquidity`, tagged **`real_ask`**, `raw_sha256` page-provenance per line. Top-of-book ONLY — ZERO per-market `/orderbook` calls (no scope-creep into the L2/Phase-2 depth lane). NOT deduped across passes (correct for a BBO time series, unlike the settlement label ledger). Honest completeness: hitting the call cap with an active cursor sets `truncated=True`/`completeness_ok=False`; nothing else lowers it. Wired into `hourly_pass.py` on `UNIVERSE_SWEEP_UTC_HOURS = {0, 6, 12, 18}` with the same `_safe_call` fault-isolation as every sibling; unlike the settlement/forecast/actuals label legs, these are FRESH live BBOs so they DO fold into n_markets/n_lines. **Live run, independently re-verified against committed tape (not just the agent's self-report):** 20 calls, 20,000 lines, all `price_source_tag: real_ask`, single `capture_id`, 0 JSON parse errors, 0 missing required fields; 7,489/20k lines carry a non-zero `yes_ask`, 2,018/20k a non-zero `volume`. `pytest`: 1167 passed (1151 prior + 16 new). `invariants --full`: green (only pre-existing non-gating L25/L74 advisories); Hard Rule #3 not tripped (prices parsed from `_dollars` and stored raw, no `yes_ask`/`no_ask` arithmetic). No strategy claim, no P&L, `kb/strategies/00-index.md` untouched — collector build, two-agent verdict rule does not apply (Q44/Q45 precedent).
**STOP-level premise finding — ESCALATED to Ryan, NOT silently forced:** the live `status=open` universe is **>80,000 markets** (probed to 80 calls; the cursor was still active at 80k), NOT the ~10k the queue assumed. So the queue's “≥95% coverage in ≤20 calls” acceptance is UNMEETABLE at the ≤20-call bound: 20×1000 reaches ≤20k = **<25% coverage**, and every live pass HONESTLY reports `truncated=True`/`completeness_ok=False`. The collector's honest-partial behavior is working exactly as designed; it is the acceptance TARGET (and its 10k premise) that is broken. **Storage bombshell (GOAL.md M3, Ryan-gated):** ~890 bytes/line × 20k = **17.8 MB per capped pass** × 4/day ≈ **~71 MB/day** — already OVER the 50 MB external-storage ceiling in a SINGLE day (and full 80k-coverage would be ~1 GB/day), vastly above the queue's projected 12 MB/day (which assumed ~3 MB/pass at ~10k markets). **Dead-tail finding:** ~63% of captured open markets have `yes_ask=0` and ~90% `volume=0` (dominated by auto-generated `KXMVESPORTSMULTIGAMEEXTENDED` multi-leg series) — a cross-sectional BBO census should filter on activity/liquidity before treating a market as a real quote. **Three Ryan design calls, NONE decided here:** (a) raise the call cap (~85+ calls to exhaust >80k at 1000/page); (b) add an activity/liquidity discovery filter to shrink both the target universe AND the storage; (c) accept a bounded partial-coverage snapshot per pass (the current honest behavior). **The leg is wired but its live {0,6,12,18} cadence is effectively gated behind the storage decision** — flagged, not switched on. **Wording divergences (documented, not forced):** (1) “verbatim BBOs” are parsed `_dollars`/`_fp` strings → floats (sibling-consistent w/ sports_pairs/settlement_ledger, invariant-safe), not raw strings; (2) the coverage cross-check “against the listing's own total count” found the listing exposes NO total field (top-level keys are just `cursor`/`markets`), so coverage is asserted by clean cursor-exhaustion, with total-count coverage wired future-proof for if Kalshi ever adds it. **Run-hygiene note for Ryan:** this run hit a background-subagent race — a delegated `collector-engineer` ran concurrently with the lead's direct build and collided on the same files (duplicate test defs, a clobbered untracked module, a 3× bloated smoke tape); resolved to a single coherent state and one clean 20k-line pass, but the lesson is: never run a background collector build concurrently with direct edits to the same files. Lesson candidates for a kb-distiller pass: correct L10's “10k+” figure to >80k; the dead-tail activity-filter rule; L90 corroboration for OPEN markets; the multi-hour-gate test-collision rule.
Status update (2026-07-21, idle-run policy (c), does NOT alter the DONE verdict): a full-history liquidity census (`scripts/universe_sweep_liquidity_census.py` over `dt=2026-07-17`..`21`, 300,000 lines / 0 malformed, all `real_ask`, NO network) now feeds Ryan design-call **(b)** ["add an activity/liquidity discovery filter"] with concrete storage-saving numbers: filtering at capture time to the ACTIVITY tier (`open_interest>0 OR volume>0`) retains only **10.74% of bytes** (~71 MB/day → ~7.6 MB/day), to FILLABLE (`yes_ask>0 AND yes_ask_size>=1`) **2.89% of bytes** (~2 MB/day), to LIQUID **2.76%** — an ~89–97% cut that drops only no-offer / no-activity artifacts (**96.97%** of the census is a dead tail, **~96.9%** of it two auto-generated multi-leg series `KXMVESPORTSMULTIGAMEEXTENDED` 82.21% + `KXMVECROSSCATEGORY` 14.68%). Confirms `volume_24h` is effectively always-zero family-wide (~5/300k rows; the L96 schema defect, across the full history). **NO code/collector change to `universe_sweep` this run** — cadence + filter stay Ryan-gated. **NOTE (2026-07-15) — take-profit / exit-timing evaluated as an EV lever, REJECTED as a source.** For a correctly-priced binary, exit timing reshapes VARIANCE but does not add EV; it adds EV only with exploitable post-entry path structure (drift/reversion), which S24 (near-close hourly-return reversion) already tested and killed DEAD-by-round-trip. S14 specifically settles intra-hour (premium capture) so there is no take-profit window at all. Do NOT re-propose take-profit/stop-loss as an EV source without a NEW path-structure finding. The real EV levers are STRUCTURAL: fee/rebate sign (Q35), fill realism (Q34), capital velocity, and selection (only trade when the wing is most overpriced) — not exit cleverness.

## Retro amendments — proposed 2026-07-05, ADOPTED 2026-07-10 (PR #18 merged)

Drafted by the weekly retro run from that week's "Log of runs". **Adopted** — Ryan merged
PR #18 on 2026-07-10T19:55:32Z, so all 3 items below are now binding protocol, not proposals.
This run (2026-07-11) already followed #1 (mandatory `git reset --hard origin/main` before
the step 0b diff) and #2 (no more `git push origin --delete` retries) and applied #3 (PR #4
is 8 days old, flagged `Priority: high` in this run's phone note). Nothing here relaxed an
invariant or a Stop rule, deleted or reordered a queue item, or touched source code.

1. **Step 0b clarification — reset local `main` before diffing stranded branches.** On
   2026-07-05T05:19Z the research run found its sandbox's local `main` ref was ~2 days stale,
   which made every `tape/hourly-*` branch look like it carried far more missing lines than it
   actually did (including in files the collector never touches) — caught before it produced
   a bad commit, but only because that run happened to check. Proposed addition to step 0b:
   run `git fetch origin main && git reset --hard origin/main` (or equivalent) immediately
   before diffing any `tape/hourly-*` branch against `main`, every run, not only when a diff
   looks suspicious.

2. **Step 0b — stop retrying the branch-delete that always fails.** Every research run since
   2026-07-03 (at least 5 runs, per the log below) has attempted `git push origin --delete` on
   fully-reconciled `tape/hourly-*` branches, and every single attempt has failed with the same
   documented cloud-session permission boundary. Proposed: stop attempting the delete each run
   — it costs a tool call and a log sentence for a guaranteed no-op — and just note
   reconciled-but-undeleted branches once per run instead. Separately, flagging for Ryan: if
   the stale branches should actually get cleaned up, the cloud GitHub App/token would need
   branch-delete scope added. That's a one-time permissions change only Ryan can make; no loop
   run can fix it from inside the sandbox.

3. **New — stuck-PR escalation after 5+ days with no owner action.** PR #4 (Q1's odds-api leg)
   has been open since 2026-07-03 waiting on Ryan to paste `ODDS_API_KEY` into the environment
   — at least 6 research runs now have silently re-noted "skipped Q1, unrelated" without ever
   escalating. Proposed: if an open PR has sat more than 5 days blocked purely on a Ryan-side
   action (a key, a decision, a merge) with no new activity, that run's ntfy phone note should
   use `Priority: high` (instead of the default) and name the specific blocking action once,
   so a stuck item doesn't stay silent indefinitely.
